<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">};</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Configure the client</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">ai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-ow">new</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">GoogleGenAI</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">apiKey</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">process</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">env</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">GEMINI_API_KEY</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Create a chat session</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">chat</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">ai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">chats</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">create</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">model</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'gemini-2.0-flash'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">config</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">chat</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">sendMessage</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">message</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'Turn this place into a party!'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Print out each of the function calls requested from this single call</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-nx">console</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">log</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"Example 1: Forced function calling"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">);</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">for</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">fn</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-k">of</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">functionCalls</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">args</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nb">Object</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">entries</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">fn</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">args</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">map</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(([</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">key</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">val</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">])</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span>&gt;<span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">${</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">key</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">${</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">val</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">        </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">join</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">', '</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">);</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">console</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">log</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">${</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">fn</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">name</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">${</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">args</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">)`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">);</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><p> Каждый из напечатанных результатов отражает один вызов функции, запрошенный моделью. Чтобы отправить результаты обратно, включите ответы в том же порядке, в котором они были запрошены.</p><p> Python SDK поддерживает функцию, называемую <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/function-calling?hl=ru#automatic_function_calling_python_only">автоматическим вызовом функции</a> , которая преобразует функцию Python в объявления, обрабатывает выполнение вызова функции и цикл ответа для вас. Ниже приведен пример для нашего варианта использования disco.</p><aside class="note"> <strong>Примечание:</strong> <span>Автоматический вызов функций на данный момент является единственной функцией Python SDK.</span> </aside><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_10" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">google</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">genai</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kn">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">google.genai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Actual implementation functions</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">def</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nf">power_disco_ball_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">power</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">bool</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">-</span>&gt; <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sd">"""Powers the spinning disco ball.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Args:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        power: Whether to turn the disco ball on or off.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Returns:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        A status dictionary indicating the current state.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    """</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">return</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"status"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-sa">f</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"Disco ball powered </span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'on'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-k">if</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">power</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-k">else</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'off'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-k">def</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nf">start_music_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">energetic</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">bool</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">loud</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">bool</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">-</span>&gt; <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sd">"""Play some music matching the specified parameters.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Args:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        energetic: Whether the music is energetic or not.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        loud: Whether the music is loud or not.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Returns:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        A dictionary containing the music settings.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    """</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">music_type</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"energetic"</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">if</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">energetic</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">else</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"chill"</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">volume</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"loud"</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">if</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">loud</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">else</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"quiet"</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">return</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"music_type"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">music_type</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"volume"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">volume</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-k">def</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nf">dim_lights_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">brightness</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">float</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">-</span>&gt; <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sd">"""Dim the lights.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Args:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        brightness: The brightness of the lights, 0.0 is off, 1.0 is full.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Returns:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        A dictionary containing the new brightness setting.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    """</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">return</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"brightness"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">brightness</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"tools"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">power_disco_ball_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">start_music_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">dim_lights_impl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">],</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">chat</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">chats</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">create</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">model</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"gemini-2.0-flash"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">response</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">chat</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">send_message</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"Do everything you need to this place into party!"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-nb">print</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-se">\n</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">Example 2: Automatic function calling"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-nb">print</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">text</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># I've turned on the disco ball, started playing loud and energetic music, and dimmed the lights to 50% brightness. Let's get this party started!</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h2 id="compositional_function_calling" data-text=" Вызов композиционной функции" tabindex="-1"> Вызов композиционной функции</h2><p> Gemini 2.0 поддерживает композиционный вызов функций, что означает, что модель может объединять несколько вызовов функций вместе. Например, чтобы ответить «Получить температуру в моем текущем местоположении», API Gemini может вызвать как функцию <code translate="no" dir="ltr">get_current_location()</code> , так и функцию <code translate="no" dir="ltr">get_weather()</code> , которая принимает местоположение в качестве параметра.</p><aside class="note"> <strong>Примечание:</strong> <span>Вызов композиционных функций в настоящее время доступен только в <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/live?hl=ru">Live API</a> . Объявление функции <code translate="no" dir="ltr">run()</code> , которое обрабатывает асинхронную настройку веб-сокета, опущено для краткости.</span> </aside><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_11" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Light control schemas</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_on_the_lights_schema</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'name'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'turn_on_the_lights'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_off_the_lights_schema</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'name'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'turn_off_the_lights'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">prompt</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"""</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">  Hey, can you write run some python code to turn on the lights, wait 10s and then turn off the lights?</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">  """</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'code_execution'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}},</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'function_declarations'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_on_the_lights_schema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_off_the_lights_schema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">run</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">modality</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"AUDIO"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section><section><h3 id="javascript_10" data-text=" JavaScript " tabindex="-1"> JavaScript </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="JavaScript"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Light control schemas</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOnTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">name</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'turn_on_the_lights'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">};</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOffTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">name</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'turn_off_the_lights'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">};</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">  Hey, can you write run some python code to turn on the lights, wait 10s and then turn off the lights?</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">codeExecution</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">},</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">functionDeclarations</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOnTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOffTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">];</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">run</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">modality</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"AUDIO"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h2 id="function_calling_modes" data-text=" Режимы вызова функций" tabindex="-1"> Режимы вызова функций</h2><p> API Gemini позволяет вам контролировать, как модель использует предоставленные инструменты (декларации функций). В частности, вы можете установить режим в <code translate="no" dir="ltr">function_calling_config</code> .</p><ul><li> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">AUTO (Default)</code> : модель решает, генерировать ли ответ на естественном языке или предлагать вызов функции на основе подсказки и контекста. Это наиболее гибкий режим, рекомендуемый для большинства сценариев.</li><li> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ANY</code> : Модель ограничена тем, чтобы всегда предсказывать вызов функции и гарантировать соответствие схеме функции. Если <code translate="no" dir="ltr">allowed_function_names</code> не указано, модель может выбирать из любого из предоставленных объявлений функций. Если <code translate="no" dir="ltr">allowed_function_names</code> указано в виде списка, модель может выбирать только из функций в этом списке. Используйте этот режим, когда требуется вызов функции в ответ на каждый запрос (если применимо).</li><li><p> <code translate="no" dir="ltr">NONE</code> : модели <em>запрещено</em> делать вызовы функций. Это эквивалентно отправке запроса без каких-либо объявлений функций. Используйте это, чтобы временно отключить вызов функций, не удаляя определения инструментов. </p></li></ul><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_12" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">google.genai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Configure function calling mode</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">tool_config</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">ToolConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">function_calling_config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">FunctionCallingConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
        <span class="devsite-syntax-n">mode</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"ANY"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">allowed_function_names</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"get_current_temperature"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Create the generation config</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">GenerateContentConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">temperature</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-mi">0</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">],</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># not defined here.</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tool_config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">tool_config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section><section><h3 id="javascript_11" data-text=" JavaScript " tabindex="-1"> JavaScript </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="JavaScript"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-k">import</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">FunctionCallingConfigMode</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kr">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'@google/genai'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Configure function calling mode</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">toolConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">functionCallingConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">mode</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">FunctionCallingConfigMode</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">ANY</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">allowedFunctionNames</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'get_current_temperature'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">};</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Create the generation config</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">temperature</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-mf">0</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// not defined here.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">toolConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">toolConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">};</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h2 id="automatic_function_calling_python_only" data-text="Автоматический вызов функций (только Python)" tabindex="-1">Автоматический вызов функций (только Python)</h2><p> При использовании Python SDK вы можете предоставлять функции Python напрямую как инструменты. SDK автоматически преобразует функцию Python в объявления, обрабатывает выполнение вызова функции и цикл ответа для вас. Затем Python SDK автоматически:</p><ol><li> Обнаруживает ответы на вызовы функций из модели.</li><li> Вызовите соответствующую функцию Python в вашем коде.</li><li> Отправляет ответ функции обратно в модель.</li><li> Возвращает окончательный текстовый ответ модели.</li></ol><p> Чтобы использовать это, определите свою функцию с подсказками типов и строкой документации, а затем передайте саму функцию (не декларацию JSON) в качестве инструмента: </p><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_13" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">google</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">genai</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kn">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">google.genai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Define the function with type hints and docstring</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">def</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nf">get_current_temperature</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">location</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">str</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">-</span>&gt; <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sd">"""Gets the current temperature for a given location.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Args:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        location: The city and state, e.g. San Francisco, CA</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    Returns:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">        A dictionary containing the temperature and unit.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sd">    """</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># ... (implementation) ...</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">return</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"temperature"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-mi">25</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"unit"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"Celsius"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Configure the client and model</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">client</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">genai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">Client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">api_key</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">os</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">getenv</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"GEMINI_API_KEY"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">))</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Replace with your actual API key setup</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">GenerateContentConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">get_current_temperature</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Pass the function itself</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Make the request</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">response</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">models</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">generate_content</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">model</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"gemini-2.0-flash"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">contents</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"What's the temperature in Boston?"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-nb">print</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">text</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># The SDK handles the function call and returns the final text</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><p> Вы можете отключить автоматический вызов функций с помощью: </p><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_14" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># To disable automatic function calling:</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">config</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">GenerateContentConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">get_current_temperature</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">],</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">automatic_function_calling</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">AutomaticFunctionCallingConfig</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">disable</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-kc">True</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h3 id="automatic_function_schema_declaration" data-text=" Декларация схемы автоматической функции" tabindex="-1"> Декларация схемы автоматической функции</h3><p> Автоматическое извлечение схемы из функций Python работает не во всех случаях. Например: оно не обрабатывает случаи, когда вы описываете поля вложенного словаря-объекта. API может описывать любой из следующих типов: </p><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_15" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-n">AllowedType</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nb">int</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">|</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">float</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">|</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">bool</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">|</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">str</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">|</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">list</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'AllowedType'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">|</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nb">str</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">AllowedType</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">])</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><p> Чтобы увидеть, как выглядит выведенная схема, вы можете преобразовать ее с помощью <a href="https://googleapis.github.io/python-genai/genai.html#genai.types.FunctionDeclaration.from_callable"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">from_callable</code></a> : </p><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_16" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-k">def</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nf">multiply</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">a</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">float</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">b</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-nb">float</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">):</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sd">"""Returns a * b."""</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">return</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">a</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">*</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">b</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">fn_decl</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">types</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">FunctionDeclaration</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">from_callable</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nb">callable</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">multiply</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># to_json_dict() provides a clean JSON representation.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-nb">print</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">fn_decl</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">to_json_dict</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">())</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h2 id="multi-tool_use_combine_native_tools_with_function_calling" data-text=" Многофункциональное использование: объединение собственных инструментов с вызовом функций" tabindex="-1"> Многофункциональное использование: объединение собственных инструментов с вызовом функций</h2><p> С Gemini 2.0 вы можете включить несколько инструментов, объединяющих собственные инструменты с вызовом функций одновременно. Вот пример, который включает два инструмента, <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/grounding?hl=ru">Grounding with Google Search</a> и <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/code-execution?hl=ru">code execution</a> , в запросе с использованием <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/live?hl=ru">Live API</a> .</p><aside class="note"> <strong>Примечание:</strong> <span>Использование нескольких инструментов в настоящее время доступно только в <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/live?hl=ru">Live API</a> . Объявление функции <code translate="no" dir="ltr">run()</code> , которая обрабатывает асинхронную настройку веб-сокета, опущено для краткости.</span> </aside><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_17" data-text=" Питон " tabindex="-1"> Питон </h3><p></p><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Multiple tasks example - combining lights, code execution, and search</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-n">prompt</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"""</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">  Hey, I need you to do three things for me.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">    1.  Turn on the lights.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">    2.  Then compute the largest prime palindrome under 100000.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">    3.  Then use Google Search to look up information about the largest earthquake in California the week of Dec 5 2024.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">  Thanks!</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-s2">  """</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'google_search'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}},</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'code_execution'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}},</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'function_declarations'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">:</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_on_the_lights_schema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">turn_off_the_lights_schema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]}</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># not defined here.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Execute the prompt with specified tools in audio modality</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">run</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">modality</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"AUDIO"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section><section><h3 id="javascript_12" data-text=" JavaScript " tabindex="-1"> JavaScript </h3><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="JavaScript"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Multiple tasks example - combining lights, code execution, and search</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">  Hey, I need you to do three things for me.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">    1.  Turn on the lights.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">    2.  Then compute the largest prime palindrome under 100000.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">    3.  Then use Google Search to look up information about the largest earthquake in California the week of Dec 5 2024.</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">  Thanks!</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">googleSearch</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">},</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">codeExecution</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">},</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">functionDeclarations</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOnTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">turnOffTheLightsSchema</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// not defined here.</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">];</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Execute the prompt with specified tools in audio modality</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">run</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">prompt</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">modality</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"AUDIO"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><p> Разработчики Python могут опробовать это в <a href="https://github.com/google-gemini/cookbook/blob/main/quickstarts/Get_started_LiveAPI_tools.ipynb">блокноте Live API Tool Use</a> .</p><h2 id="model_context_protocol_mcp" data-text=" Модель контекстного протокола (MCP)" tabindex="-1"> Модель контекстного протокола (MCP)</h2><p> <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/introduction">Model Context Protocol (MCP)</a> — открытый стандарт для подключения приложений ИИ к внешним инструментам и данным. MCP предоставляет общий протокол для моделей для доступа к контексту, такому как функции (инструменты), источники данных (ресурсы) или предопределенные подсказки.</p><p> Gemini SDK имеют встроенную поддержку MCP, что сокращает шаблонный код и предлагает <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/function-calling?hl=ru#automatic_function_calling_python_only">автоматический вызов инструментов</a> для инструментов MCP. Когда модель генерирует вызов инструмента MCP, клиентский SDK Python и JavaScript может автоматически выполнить инструмент MCP и отправить ответ обратно модели в последующем запросе, продолжая этот цикл до тех пор, пока модель не перестанет делать вызовы инструментов.</p><p> Здесь вы можете найти пример использования локального сервера MCP с Gemini и <code translate="no" dir="ltr">mcp</code> SDK. </p><div class="ds-selector-tabs" data-ds-scope="code-sample"><section><h3 id="python_18" data-text=" Питон" tabindex="-1"> Питон</h3><p> Убедитесь, что на выбранной вами платформе установлена ​​последняя версия <a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/introduction"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">mcp</code> SDK</a> . </p><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Bash"><code translate="no" dir="ltr">pip<span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span>install<span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span>mcp
</code></pre></devsite-code><aside class="note"> <strong>Примечание:</strong> <span>Python поддерживает автоматический вызов инструмента, передавая <code translate="no" dir="ltr">ClientSession</code> в параметры <code translate="no" dir="ltr">tools</code> . Если вы хотите отключить его, вы можете предоставить <code translate="no" dir="ltr">automatic_function_calling</code> с отключенным <code translate="no" dir="ltr">True</code> .</span> </aside><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="Python"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-kn">import</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nn">os</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-n">server_params</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">StdioServerParameters</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">command</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"npx"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Executable</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">args</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"-y"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"@philschmid/weather-mcp"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">],</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># MCP Server</span>
    <span class="devsite-syntax-n">env</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-kc">None</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>  <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Optional environment variables</span>

    <span class="devsite-syntax-k">async</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">with</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">stdio_client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">server_params</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-k">as</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">read</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-n">write</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">):</span>

            <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Prompt to get the weather for the current day in London.</span>
            <span class="devsite-syntax-n">prompt</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span> <span class="devsite-syntax-sa">f</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"What is the weather in London in </span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">datetime</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">now</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">()</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-n">strftime</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'%Y-%m-</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">%d</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">?"</span>
            <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Initialize the connection between client and server</span>

            <span class="devsite-syntax-c1"># Send request to the model with MCP function declarations</span>

                <span class="devsite-syntax-n">model</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"gemini-2.0-flash"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>

</code></pre></devsite-code><aside class="note"> <strong>Примечание:</strong> <span>JavaScript поддерживает автоматический вызов инструмента, оборачивая <code translate="no" dir="ltr">client</code> с помощью <code translate="no" dir="ltr">mcpToTool</code> . Если вы хотите отключить его, вы можете предоставить <code translate="no" dir="ltr">automaticFunctionCalling</code> с отключенным <code translate="no" dir="ltr">true</code> .</span> </aside><div></div><devsite-code><pre class="devsite-click-to-copy" translate="no" dir="ltr" is-upgraded syntax="JavaScript"><code translate="no" dir="ltr"><span class="devsite-syntax-k">import</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">GoogleGenAI</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">FunctionCallingConfigMode</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">mcpToTool</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kr">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s1">'@google/genai'</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">import</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">Client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kr">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/index.js"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">import</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">StdioClientTransport</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-kr">from</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/stdio.js"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">;</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Create server parameters for stdio connection</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">serverParams</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-ow">new</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">StdioClientTransport</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">command</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"npx"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Executable</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">args</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"-y"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"@philschmid/weather-mcp"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">]</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// MCP Server</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-ow">new</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">Client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">name</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"example-client"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">version</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"1.0.0"</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">}</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">);</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Configure the client</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">ai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-ow">new</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">GoogleGenAI</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">apiKey</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">process</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">env</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">GEMINI_API_KEY</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Initialize the connection between client and server</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">connect</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">serverParams</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">);</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Send request to the model with MCP tools</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-kd">const</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">=</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">ai</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">models</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">generateContent</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">({</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">model</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-s2">"gemini-2.0-flash"</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">contents</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">`What is the weather in London in </span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">${</span><span class="devsite-syntax-ow">new</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nb">Date</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">().</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">toLocaleDateString</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">()</span><span class="devsite-syntax-si">}</span><span class="devsite-syntax-sb">?`</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">config</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">{</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">tools</span><span class="devsite-syntax-o">:</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">[</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">mcpToTool</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)],</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// uses the session, will automatically call the tool</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Uncomment if you **don't** want the sdk to automatically call the tool</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// automaticFunctionCalling: {</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">//   disable: true,</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">    </span><span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// },</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-w">  </span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">},</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-p">});</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-nx">console</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">log</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">(</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">response</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">text</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">)</span>

<span class="devsite-syntax-c1">// Close the connection</span>
<span class="devsite-syntax-k">await</span><span class="devsite-syntax-w"> </span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">client</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">.</span><span class="devsite-syntax-nx">close</span><span class="devsite-syntax-p">();</span>
</code></pre></devsite-code></section></div><h3 id="limitations_with_built-in_mcp_support" data-text="Ограничения при встроенной поддержке MCP" tabindex="-1">Ограничения при встроенной поддержке MCP</h3><p> Встроенная поддержка MCP является <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/models?hl=ru#preview">экспериментальной</a> функцией в наших SDK и имеет следующие ограничения:</p><ul><li> Поддерживаются только инструменты, а не ресурсы или подсказки.</li><li> Он доступен для Python и JavaScript/TypeScript SDK.</li><li> В будущих версиях могут произойти критические изменения.</li></ul><p> Ручная интеграция серверов MCP всегда возможна, если это ограничивает ваши возможности.</p><h2 id="supported_models" data-text=" Поддерживаемые модели" tabindex="-1"> Поддерживаемые модели</h2><p> Экспериментальные модели не включены. Их возможности вы можете найти на странице <a href="https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/models?hl=ru">обзора моделей</a> .</p><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align: left"> Модель</th><th style="text-align: left"> Вызов функции</th><th style="text-align: left"> Параллельный вызов функций</th><th style="text-align: left"> Вызов композиционной функции</br> (Только API в реальном времени)</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: left"> Близнецы 2.0 Флэш</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: left"> Gemini 2.0 Flash-Lite</td><td style="text-align: left"> Х</td><td style="text-align: left"> Х</td><td style="text-align: left"> Х</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: left"> Близнецы 1.5 Флэш</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: left"> Близнецы 1.5 Про</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td><td style="text-align: left"> ✔️</td></tr></tbody></table><h2 id="best_practices" data-text=" Лучшие практики" tabindex="-1"> Лучшие практики</h2><ul><li> <strong>Описания функций и параметров:</strong> будьте предельно ясны и конкретны в своих описаниях. Модель опирается на них, чтобы выбрать правильную функцию и предоставить соответствующие аргументы.</li><li> <strong>Именование:</strong> используйте описательные имена функций (без пробелов, точек и тире).</li><li> <strong>Строгая типизация:</strong> используйте определенные типы (целое число, строка, перечисление) для параметров, чтобы уменьшить количество ошибок. Если параметр имеет ограниченный набор допустимых значений, используйте перечисление.</li><li> <strong>Выбор инструмента:</strong> Хотя модель может использовать произвольное количество инструментов, предоставление слишком большого количества может увеличить риск выбора неправильного или неоптимального инструмента. Для достижения наилучших результатов стремитесь предоставлять только соответствующие инструменты для контекста или задачи, в идеале сохраняя активный набор максимум в 10-20. Рассмотрите динамический выбор инструментов на основе контекста разговора, если у вас большое общее количество инструментов.</li><li> <strong>Оперативное проектирование:</strong><ul><li> Предоставьте контекст: расскажите модели о ее роли (например, «Вы полезный помощник по прогнозу погоды»).</li><li> Дайте инструкции: укажите, как и когда использовать функции (например, «Не угадывайте даты; всегда используйте будущую дату для прогнозов»).</li><li> Поощряйте уточнения: попросите модель задавать уточняющие вопросы при необходимости.</li></ul></li><li> <strong>Температура:</strong> используйте низкую температуру (например, 0) для более детерминированных и надежных вызовов функций.</li><li> <strong>Проверка:</strong> если вызов функции имеет существенные последствия (например, размещение заказа), проверьте вызов у ​​пользователя перед его выполнением.</li><li> <strong>Обработка ошибок</strong> : реализуйте надежную обработку ошибок в своих функциях, чтобы изящно обрабатывать неожиданные входные данные или сбои API. Возвращайте информативные сообщения об ошибках, которые модель может использовать для генерации полезных ответов пользователю.</li><li> <strong>Безопасность:</strong> Помните о безопасности при вызове внешних API. Используйте соответствующие механизмы аутентификации и авторизации. Избегайте раскрытия конфиденциальных данных при вызовах функций.</li><li> <strong>Ограничения по токенам:</strong> Описания функций и параметры учитываются в вашем лимите входных токенов. Если вы достигаете лимитов по токенам, рассмотрите возможность ограничения количества функций или длины описаний, разбейте сложные задачи на более мелкие, более целевые наборы функций.</li></ul><h2 id="notes_and_limitations" data-text=" Примечания и ограничения" tabindex="-1"> Примечания и ограничения</h2><ul><li> Поддерживается только <a href="https://ai.google.dev/api/caching?hl=ru#FunctionDeclaration">подмножество схемы OpenAPI</a> .</li><li> Поддерживаемые типы параметров в Python ограничены.</li><li> Автоматический вызов функций доступен только в Python SDK. </li></ul><link href="https://ai.google.dev/site-assets/css/style.css?v=3&hl=ru" rel="stylesheet" data-page-link><link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Google+Symbols:opsz,wght,FILL,GRAD@20..48,100..700,0..1,-50..200" rel="stylesheet" data-page-link>
  

  
</div>
